f1.x ? -1 : 1; // Push apart if (rectsOverlap(f1,f2)) { const push=2; if(f1.xb.x && a.yb.y; } function checkAttack(att,def) { if (!att.attacking || att.attackTimer < (att.attackType===0?10:15)) return; if (def.hitCooldown>0) return; const range = att.attackType===2?130:(att.attackType===1?90:65); const dx = Math.abs((att.x+att.w/2)-(def.x+def.w/2)); const dy = Math.abs((att.y+att.h/2)-(def.y+def.h/2)); if (dxf.remove(),150); } function spawnParticles(x,y,color) { const arena=document.getElementById('arena'); const sx=canvas.clientWidth/canvas.width, sy=canvas.clientHeight/canvas.height; for(let i=0;i<8;i++){ const p=document.createElement('div'); p.className='particle'; const angle=(Math.PI*2*i)/8, dist=35+Math.random()*40; p.style.cssText=`width:${4+Math.random()*5}px;height:${4+Math.random()*5}px;background:${color};left:${x*sx}px;top:${y*sy}px;--tx:${Math.cos(angle)*dist}px;--ty:${Math.sin(angle)*dist}px;box-shadow:0 0 6px ${color};`; arena.appendChild(p); setTimeout(()=>p.remove(),800); } } function updateBars() { const [f1,f2]=fighters; document.getElementById('hp1-bar').style.width=(f1.hp/MAX_HP*100)+'%'; document.getElementById('hp2-bar').style.width=(f2.hp/MAX_HP*100)+'%'; document.getElementById('sp1-bar').style.width=(f1.sp/MAX_SP*100)+'%'; document.getElementById('sp2-bar').style.width=(f2.sp/MAX_SP*100)+'%'; } function endRound() { if (gameState!=='fighting') return; gameState='roundEnd'; clearInterval(timerInterval); const [f1,f2]=fighters; let w=null; if(f1.hp<=0&&f2.hp<=0) w=null; else if(f1.hp<=0||(timeLeft<=0&&f2.hp>f1.hp)) w=2; else if(f2.hp<=0||(timeLeft<=0&&f1.hp>f2.hp)) w=1; if(w===1) p1Wins++; else if(w===2) p2Wins++; const koText = w?'K.O.!':'DRAW!'; const koColor = w===1?'#00d4ff':w===2?'#ff6a00':'#ffffff'; if(p1Wins>=2||p2Wins>=2){ setTimeout(()=>{ showOverlay(koText, koColor, 1300, ()=>{ const wChar = p1Wins>=2 ? p1Char : p2Char; const wLabel = p1Wins>=2 ? 'Player 1' : 'Player 2'; p1Wins=0; p2Wins=0; round=1; document.getElementById('winner-name').textContent=wChar.name.toUpperCase(); document.getElementById('winner-name').style.color=wChar.color; document.getElementById('winner-game-tag').textContent=wChar.game; document.getElementById('win-char-img').src=wChar.src; document.getElementById('win-char-img').style.filter=`drop-shadow(0 0 30px ${wChar.color})`; document.getElementById('win-label').textContent=wLabel+' Wins!'; showScreen('win-screen'); }); },300); } else { round++; setTimeout(()=>{ showOverlay(koText, koColor, 1200, ()=>{ fighters[0].hp=MAX_HP; fighters[1].hp=MAX_HP; fighters[0].sp=0; fighters[1].sp=0; fighters[0].x=Math.round(canvas.width*0.13); fighters[1].x=Math.round(canvas.width*0.75); fighters[0].y=GROUND_Y-fighters[0].h; fighters[1].y=GROUND_Y-fighters[1].h; timeLeft=60; document.getElementById('round-display').textContent='Round '+round; showOverlay('ROUND '+round,'#00d4ff',1200,()=>{ showOverlay('FIGHT!','#ff6a00',800,()=>{ gameState='fighting'; startTimer(); }); }); }); },400); } } // ── AI BRAIN ── let _aiTimer = 0; let _aiAction = null; // current planned action let _aiJumpCooldown = 0; let _aiAttackCooldown = 0; function updateAI(aiFighter, target) { if (gameState !== 'fighting') return; const af = fighters[aiFighter]; const tf = fighters[1 - aiFighter]; const spd = 3.8 + (af.char.stats.speed - 3) * 0.45; const dx = tf.x - af.x; // positive = target is to the right const dist = Math.abs(dx); const facingRight = dx > 0; _aiTimer--; _aiJumpCooldown--; _aiAttackCooldown--; // ── Think every ~25 frames ── if (_aiTimer <= 0) { _aiTimer = 20 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 20); // Decide next action const roll = Math.random(); if (dist > 160) { // Far away → chase _aiAction = 'chase'; } else if (dist < 55) { // Very close → attack or back off if (roll < 0.55) _aiAction = 'attack'; else if (roll < 0.7) _aiAction = 'retreat'; else _aiAction = 'jump_attack'; } else { // Mid range if (roll < 0.4) _aiAction = 'chase'; else if (roll < 0.65) _aiAction = 'attack'; else if (roll < 0.8) _aiAction = 'jump'; else _aiAction = 'idle'; } } // ── Execute action ── af.vx = 0; // reset horizontal // Always face the target af.facing = facingRight ? -1 : 1; switch (_aiAction) { case 'chase': af.vx = facingRight ? spd : -spd; break; case 'retreat': af.vx = facingRight ? -spd : spd; break; case 'attack': // Move slightly toward target and punch/kick if (dist > 70) af.vx = facingRight ? spd : -spd; if (!af.attacking && _aiAttackCooldown <= 0) { _aiAttackCooldown = 25 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 20); const atk = Math.random(); if (atk < 0.5) { af.attacking=true; af.attackType=0; af.attackTimer=20; } else if (atk < 0.8) { af.attacking=true; af.attackType=1; af.attackTimer=30; } else if (af.sp >= MAX_SP) { af.attacking=true; af.attackType=2; af.attackTimer=45; af.special=true; af.sp=0; } else { af.attacking=true; af.attackType=0; af.attackTimer=20; } } break; case 'jump': if (af.onGround && _aiJumpCooldown <= 0) { af.vy = JUMP_FORCE; af.onGround = false; _aiJumpCooldown = 50; } break; case 'jump_attack': if (af.onGround && _aiJumpCooldown <= 0) { af.vy = JUMP_FORCE; af.onGround = false; _aiJumpCooldown = 55; } if (!af.attacking && _aiAttackCooldown <= 0) { _aiAttackCooldown = 20; af.attacking = true; af.attackType = 0; af.attackTimer = 20; } af.vx = facingRight ? spd * 0.6 : -spd * 0.6; break; default: // idle break; } // Special move if bar is full (occasional) if (af.sp >= MAX_SP && !af.attacking && Math.random() < 0.015) { af.attacking=true; af.attackType=2; af.attackTimer=45; af.special=true; af.sp=0; } } // ── RENDER ── function render() { if(!ctx) return; const } if (window._bgImg.complete && window._bgImg.naturalWidth > 0) { ctx.drawImage(window._bgImg, 0, 0, W, H); ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.25)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H); } else { ctx.fillStyle = '#0e0805'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H); } // Ground glow ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.3)'; ctx.fillRect(0,GROUND_Y,W,H-GROUND_Y); // Ground line const gLine=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,W,0); gLine.addColorStop(0,'#00d4ff'); gLine.addColorStop(0.5,'rgba(255,255,255,0.8)'); gLine.addColorStop(1,'#ff6a00'); ctx.fillStyle=gLine; ctx.fillRect(0,GROUND_Y,W,2); // Fighters fighters.forEach(f=>drawFighter(f)); } /* ── OFFSCREEN CANVAS CACHE for black-BG removal ── */ const _imgCache = new Map(); function getScreenImg(img, tintColor) { const key = img.src.slice(-20) + tintColor; if (_imgCache.has(key)) return _imgCache.get(key); if (!img.complete || !img.naturalWidth) return null; const oc = document.createElement('canvas'); oc.width = img.naturalWidth; oc.height = img.naturalHeight; const octx = oc.getContext('2d'); octx.drawImage(img, 0, 0); // Remove black: multiply each pixel — keep bright pixels, drop near-black const id = octx.getImageData(0,0,oc.width,oc.height); const d = id.data; for (let i=0; i 0.5) { // Walk cycle la = 0.55 * Math.sin(t); ra = -0.55 * Math.sin(t); ll = -0.5 * Math.sin(t); rl = 0.5 * Math.sin(t); bodyBob = Math.abs(Math.sin(t * 2)) * 3; bodyLean = 0.06 * Math.sin(t); } else { // Idle breathe const breathe = Math.sin(Date.now()*0.002) * 0.05; la = 0.15 + breathe; ra = -0.15 + breathe; bodyBob = Math.sin(Date.now()*0.002) * 1.5; } return { la, ra, ll, rl, bodyLean, bodyBob }; } function drawLimb(octx, x1, y1, angle, len, thickness, color, hasFist=false) { octx.save(); octx.translate(x1, y1); octx.rotate(angle); octx.strokeStyle = color; octx.lineWidth = thickness; octx.lineCap = 'round'; octx.beginPath(); octx.moveTo(0, 0); octx.lineTo(0, len); octx.stroke(); if (hasFist) { octx.fillStyle = color; octx.beginPath(); octx.arc(0, len, thickness*0.9, 0, Math.PI*2); octx.fill(); } octx.restore(); } function drawStickFighter(f, sx, sy) { // Fallback animated stick figure when image not available const c = f.char.color; const { la, ra, ll, rl, bodyLean, bodyBob } = getLimbAngles(f); const h = f.h, scale = h / 140; ctx.save(); const cx = f.x + f.w/2 + sx; const cy = f.y + sy + bodyBob; ctx.translate(cx, cy); ctx.scale(f.facing, 1); ctx.rotate(bodyLean); const headR = 14 * scale; const torsoL = 38 * scale; const armL = 30 * scale; const legL = 36 * scale; const thick = 5 * scale; const headY = 10 * scale; const shoulderY = headY + headR * 1.8; const hipY = shoulderY + torsoL; // glow on special if (f.special && f.attacking) { ctx.shadowBlur=30; ctx.shadowColor=c; } // Legs (behind body) drawLimb(ctx, 0, hipY, ll + Math.PI/12, legL, thick, c); drawLimb(ctx, 0, hipY, rl - Math.PI/12, legL, thick, c); // Torso ctx.strokeStyle = c; ctx.lineWidth = thick * 1.2; ctx.lineCap = 'round'; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, shoulderY); ctx.lineTo(0, hipY); ctx.stroke(); // Arms drawLimb(ctx, 0, shoulderY, la - Math.PI/10, armL, thick, c, true); drawLimb(ctx, 0, shoulderY, ra + Math.PI/10, armL, thick, c, true); // Head if (f.hitAnim > 0) { ctx.shadowBlur=20; ctx.shadowColor='#fff'; } ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(0, headY, headR, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle = c; ctx.fill(); ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.3)'; ctx.lineWidth=1; ctx.stroke(); ctx.restore(); } function drawFighter(f) { let sx=0, sy=0; if(f.hitAnim>0){sx=(Math.random()-0.5)*8; sy=(Math.random()-0.5)*4;} const { la, ra, ll, rl, bodyLean, bodyBob } = getLimbAngles(f); // Ground shadow first ctx.save(); ctx.translate(f.x+f.w/2+sx, GROUND_Y); ctx.scale(1, 0.2); const sg=ctx.createRadialGradient(0,0,0,0,0,f.w*0.6); sg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)'); sg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)'); ctx.fillStyle=sg; ctx.beginPath();ctx.ellipse(0,0,f.w*0.6,18,0,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill(); ctx.restore(); const imgReady = f.img && f.img.complete && f.img.naturalWidth > 0; if (imgReady) { // ── IMAGE-BASED FIGHTER with animated overlaid limbs ── const processedImg = getScreenImg(f.img, f.char.color); if (!processedImg) { drawStickFighter(f, sx, sy); return; } const scale = f.h / processedImg.height; const dw = processedImg.width * scale; const h = f.h; ctx.save(); const cx = f.x + f.w/2 + sx; const cy = f.y + sy + bodyBob; ctx.translate(cx, cy); ctx.scale(f.facing, 1); ctx.rotate(bodyLean); // Draw processed (black-removed) image if (f.hitAnim > 0) ctx.filter = 'brightness(4) saturate(0)'; if (f.special && f.attacking) { ctx.shadowBlur=40; ctx.shadowColor=f.char.color; } ctx.drawImage(processedImg, -dw/2, 0, dw, h); ctx.filter = 'none'; ctx.shadowBlur = 0; // Overlay animated limbs on top of the image for motion feel const c = f.char.color + 'cc'; // semi-transparent const s = h / 140; const shoulderY = h * 0.28; const hipY = h * 0.55; const armLen = h * 0.22; const legLen = h * 0.26; const lThick = 6 * s; // Attack effect glow orb if (f.attacking && f.attackTimer > (f.attackType===2?20:8)) { const range = f.attackType===2?130:(f.attackType===1?90:65); const radius = f.attackType===2?32:(f.attackType===1?24:16); const aGrad=ctx.createRadialGradient(range*0.6*s, h*0.35,0, range*0.6*s, h*0.35, radius*s); aGrad.addColorStop(0,f.char.color+'ff'); aGrad.addColorStop(1,f.char.color+'00'); ctx.fillStyle=aGrad; ctx.shadowBlur=25; ctx.shadowColor=f.char.color; ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(range*0.6*s, h*0.35, radius*s,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill(); ctx.shadowBlur=0; } // Animated arm overlays ctx.globalAlpha = 0.72; drawLimb(ctx, -dw*0.08, shoulderY, la - Math.PI/10, armLen, lThick, c, true); drawLimb(ctx, dw*0.08, shoulderY, ra + Math.PI/10, armLen, lThick, c, true); // Animated leg overlays drawLimb(ctx, -dw*0.07, hipY, ll + Math.PI/12, legLen, lThick, c); drawLimb(ctx, dw*0.07, hipY, rl - Math.PI/12, legLen, lThick, c); ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.restore(); } else { // fallback stick figure drawStickFighter(f, sx, sy); } // Neon name tag above fighter ctx.save(); ctx.font = `bold ${Math.round(f.h*0.09)}px Orbitron,sans-serif`; ctx.fillStyle = f.char.color; ctx.globalAlpha = 0.7; ctx.textAlign = 'center'; const tagX = f.x + f.w/2 + sx; const tagY = f.y + sy - 6; ctx.shadowBlur = 8; ctx.shadowColor = f.char.color; ctx.fillText(f.char.name.toUpperCase(), tagX, tagY); ctx.shadowBlur = 0; ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.restore(); } // ── INIT ── buildCards(); // Tip text document.getElementById('fight-btn').title = 'Left-click a card = P1 selects | Right-click = P2 selects'; // ── TOUCH CONTROLS ── function isMobile() { return ('ontouchstart' in window) || (navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0); } function setupTouchControls() { // Show touch pad always (it's hidden via CSS on desktop) document.getElementById('touch-controls').classList.add('visible'); // Map: [elementId, keyName, isToggle] const bindings = [ ['t-p1-left', 'a', false], ['t-p1-right', 'd', false], ['t-p1-jump', 'w', false], ['t-p1-punch', 'g', true], ['t-p1-kick', 'h', true], ['t-p1-special', 'j', true], ['t-p2-left', 'ArrowLeft', false], ['t-p2-right', 'ArrowRight', false], ['t-p2-jump', 'ArrowUp', false], ['t-p2-punch', 'n', true], ['t-p2-kick', 'm', true], ['t-p2-special', 'l', true], ]; bindings.forEach(([id, key, isToggle]) => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (!el) return; if (isToggle) { // For attack buttons: fire once per tap (simulate keydown then immediate keyup) el.addEventListener('touchstart', e => { e.preventDefault(); keys[key] = true; el.classList.add('pressed'); setTimeout(() => { keys[key] = false; el.classList.remove('pressed'); }, 120); }, { passive: false }); // Also support mouse for testing on desktop el.addEventListener('mousedown', e => { e.preventDefault(); keys[key] = true; el.classList.add('pressed'); setTimeout(() => { keys[key] = false; el.classList.remove('pressed'); }, 120); }); } else { // For movement/jump: hold = key held const press = e => { e.preventDefault(); keys[key] = true; el.classList.add('pressed'); }; const release = e => { e.preventDefault(); keys[key] = false; el.classList.remove('pressed'); }; el.addEventListener('touchstart', press, { passive: false }); el.addEventListener('touchend', release, { passive: false }); el.addEventListener('touchcancel', release, { passive: false }); el.addEventListener('mousedown', press); el.addEventListener('mouseup', release); el.addEventListener('mouseleave', release); } }); } setupTouchControls(); // Resize canvas when screen rotates or resizes function resizeCanvas() { if (!canvas) return; const arena = document.getElementById('arena'); canvas.width = arena.clientWidth || 800; canvas.height = arena.clientHeight || 360; GROUND_Y = canvas.height - 75; if (fighters.length === 2) { fighters[0].y = Math.min(fighters[0].y, GROUND_Y - fighters[0].h); fighters[1].y = Math.min(fighters[1].y, GROUND_Y - fighters[1].h); } } window.addEventListener('resize', resizeCanvas); window.addEventListener('orientationchange', () => setTimeout(resizeCanvas, 300));
